***впору.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впору.html>впо́ру</a> (13016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>по́ру</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póru</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впору.html>впо́ру</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpóru</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fitting just right
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>прийти́сь</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:оказаться.html>оказа́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:впору.html>впо́ру</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ/prijtísʹ/okazátʹsja <b>vpóru</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fit; be the right size (for)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> one might as well, one can do little more than
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впору.html>впо́ру</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:четвереньки.html>четвере́ньках</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ползти.html>ползти́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpóru</b> na četverénʹkax polztí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one might as well crawl on all fours</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вки</a>: <b>в-при-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-прыж-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-к-у</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<ol><li>for future use, in reserve, in store</li>
<li>to one's benefit

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>пряму́ю</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamúju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, feminine accusative singular of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прямой.html>прямо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjamój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straight, direct</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> straight, frankly, like it is

***враг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:враг.html>враг</a> (608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">врагъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vragŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vorgъ</i>. Compare the inherited doublet <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">во́рог</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vórog</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enemy, foe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.

***вражда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вражда.html>вражда́</a> (11336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>An Old Church Slavonicism, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*voržьda</i> (the Old East Slavic form is found in the poetic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ворожда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vorožda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vorgъ</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьda</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">wróżda</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">vražda</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вражда.html>вражда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vraždá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вражда.html>вражды́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>enmity, hostility, animosity, antagonism <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">hostile or unfriendly disposition</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:враждовать.html>враждова́ть</a> (14281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***враз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:враз.html>враз</a> (8474)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:враз.html>враз</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vraz</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> all together, simultaneously</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> immediately, at once, straight away</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вразвалку.html>вразва́лку</a> (29144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развал.html>разва́л</a>(ивать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvál(ivatʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ку</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ku</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вперемешку.html>впереме́шку</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vpereméšku</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вразвалку.html>вразва́лку</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vrazválku</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in a waddling manner, shifting one's weight from one leg to the other
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1885</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%95%D0%B3%D0%B5%D1%80%D1%8C_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Егерь (Чехов)"><a href = vnd.unilang:егерь.html>Е́герь</a></a>  | <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Huntsman_(short_story)" class="extiw" title="s:The Huntsman (short story)">The Huntsman</a> | ”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Constance_Garnett" class="extiw" title="w:Constance Garnett">Constance Garnett</a>, transl., <cite>The Witch and other stories</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>По</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:край.html>кра́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:узкоплечий.html>узкопле́чий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужчина.html>мужчи́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>сорока́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубаха.html>руба́хе</a>, ла́таных госпо́дских <a href = vnd.unilang:штаны.html>штана́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больши́х</a> <a href = krásnoj rubáxe, látanyx gospódskix štanáx i v bolʹšíx sapogáx.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">At the edge of the clearing a tall, narrow-shouldered man of forty in a red shirt, in patched trousers that had been a gentleman's, and in high boots, was slouching along with a lazy, <b>shambling</b> step.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sprawling, with arms and legs stretched out
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1884</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  chapter 3, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%94%D1%80%D0%B0%D0%BC%D0%B0_%D0%BD%D0%B0_%D0%BE%D1%85%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%B5_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)/3" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Драма на охоте (Чехов)/3"><a href = vnd.unilang:драма.html>Дра́ма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́те</a></a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Shooting_Party_(Chekhov_novel)" class="extiw" title="w:The Shooting Party (Chekhov novel)">The Shooting Party</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иду́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a>… <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>Там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнатах</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:диван.html>дива́нах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковра́х</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спя́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вразвалку.html>вразва́лку</a></b> изнеможённые, зае́зженные <a href = vnd.unilang:певец.html>певцы́</a>...</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja idú v dom… Tam vo vsex kómnatax, na divánax i kovráx, spjat <b>vrazválku</b> iznemožónnyje, zajézžennyje pevcý...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I go into the house.
